The building is a former hotel converted to apartments mostly inhabited by 20 to 30 somethings. It is across the highway from DTLA and is very convenient to get around town. We had a bit of a difficult time getting the front door unlocked a few times with the key provided but eventually got in every time. Overall the apartment was good for a few days stay for the two of us wanting to be near downtown, Koreatown, and Mid City. *When using the elevator from the lower garage level push both down and up buttons because it will not respond if you push only up (we learned after a 5 - 10 minute confused wait).</p><span data-reactid="922">Martha</span><span data-reactid="923">2016-06-12T00:00:00Z</span></li>

If this is not the location you had in mind, please search for Beverly Hills, Hollywood, Santa Monica or whatever other city you are really interested in. Los Angeles is a huge place so if it's your first time to visit, do searches of distances between sights in the greater Los Angeles area to get a realistic idea of how much time you will need to get around to really see all you want to see, especially if you will be using public transport only. You might want to consider staying for a shorter time in different areas or renting a car to get around like most Angelinos. We want guests who are happy to come to our vibrant neighborhood and are realistic in their expectations of Los Angeles. Thank you!
